            <!-- ngIf: true --><li class="top-nav-link ml-auto ng-scope" id="quick-find-external-trigger" ng-if="true" ng-init="active = false" data-hint="quick_search_intro">
    <a href="javascript:;" onclick="document.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('toggleQuickFind'))" class="ripple">
        <!-- ngIf: !active --><span class="d-flex align-items-center ng-scope" ng-if="!active">
            <svg><use href="/cachedStatic/iconUrl1?file=%2Fthemes%2Fmpa%2Fassets%2Fsvg%2Fcommon-svg%2Ficons-sprite.svg&amp;hash=qhdR2R0QVhhpU_2uFWEE#magnifier"></use></svg>        </span><!-- end ngIf: !active -->
        <!-- ngIf: active -->
    </a>
    <span class="top-tooltip">Quick Find F</span>
    <script>
        // ng-if="true" makes Angular insert a CLONE of this <li>, so this inline
        // script executes twice (parse-time + clone-insert). The IIFE keeps the
        // declarations function-scoped (no "already declared" redeclaration crash)
        // and the window guard registers the document listeners only once.
        (function () {
            if (window.__quickFindTriggerInit) { return; }
            window.__quickFindTriggerInit = true;

            let quickFindHintDemo = false;
            const setQuickFindActive = value => {
                const $scope = angular.element('#quick-find-external-trigger')?.scope();
                $scope?.$apply?.(() => {
                    $scope.active = value;
                });
            };
            // While a contextual hint is demoing Quick Find it holds the search open but
            // wants the trigger to keep showing the magnifier (not the X) — the bubble
            // points at a magnifier. The hint engine brackets the demo with this event.
            document.addEventListener('quickFindHintDemo', e => {
                quickFindHintDemo = !!e.detail;
                if (quickFindHintDemo) {
                    setQuickFindActive(false);
                }
            });
            document.addEventListener('quickFindStateChanged', e => {
                setQuickFindActive(quickFindHintDemo ? false : e.detail);
            });
        })();
    </script>
</li><!-- end ngIf: true -->

<script>
  $(function () {
    const observer = new MutationObserver(mutationsList => {
      for (const mutation of mutationsList) {
        if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
          $.cookie('chatButtonVisible', mutation.target.style.display === 'none' ? 'false' : 'true', { path: '/' });
        }
      }
    });

    observer.observe(
      document.querySelector('.top-nav-link.chat'),
      {
        attributes: true,
        attributeFilter: [ 'style' ],
      },
    );
  });
</script>

<script type="text/ng-template" id="notification-panel-default-tpl.html">
    <div
    class="sd-notification-panel-item notif-row"
    ng-class="{
        'notif-row--unread': notification.read == 0,
        'notif-row--sticky': notification.sticky == 1,
        'notif-row--actions-visible': isActiveActionRow()
    }"
>
    <div class="notif-row__avatar" ng-if="notification.userAvatar" ng-bind-html="notification.userAvatar | trustSvg"></div>
    <div class="notif-row__avatar notif-row__avatar--fallback" ng-if="!notification.userAvatar">
        {{notification.senderDisplayName.charAt(0)}}
    </div>

    <div class="notif-row__body" ng-click="navigateTo(); $event.stopPropagation();">
        <div class="notif-row__sender">{{notification.senderDisplayName}}</div>
        <div class="notif-row__subject">{{notification.subject}}</div>
        <div class="notif-row__text">{{notification.text}}</div>
    </div>

    <div class="notif-row__corner" aria-label="Notification Options" ng-click="toggleActionRow(); $event.stopPropagation();">
        <svg class="notif-row__type-icon" aria-hidden="true">
            <use ng-attr-href="/cachedStatic/iconUrl1?file=%2Fthemes%2Fmpa%2Fassets%2Fsvg%2Fcommon-svg%2Ficons-sprite.svg&hash=qhdR2R0QVhhpU_2uFWEE#{{getTypeIcon(notification.type)}}"></use>
        </svg>

        <div class="notif-row__actions">
            <button
                type="button"
                class="notif-row__action"
                ng-show="notification.read == 1"
                ng-click="$event.stopPropagation(); toggleReadValue();"
                data-toggle="tooltip"
                data-placement="top"
                title="Mark as Unread"
                aria-label="Mark as Unread"
            >
                <svg aria-hidden="true"><use href="/cachedStatic/iconUrl1?file=%2Fthemes%2Fmpa%2Fassets%2Fsvg%2Fcommon-svg%2Ficons-sprite.svg&hash=qhdR2R0QVhhpU_2uFWEE#mail-warning"></use></svg>            </button>
            <button
                type="button"
                class="notif-row__action"
                ng-show="notification.read == 0"
                ng-click="$event.stopPropagation(); toggleReadValue();"
                data-toggle="tooltip"
                data-placement="top"
                title="Mark as Read"
                aria-label="Mark as Read"
            >
                <svg aria-hidden="true"><use href="/cachedStatic/iconUrl1?file=%2Fthemes%2Fmpa%2Fassets%2Fsvg%2Fcommon-svg%2Ficons-sprite.svg&hash=qhdR2R0QVhhpU_2uFWEE#mail-check"></use></svg>            </button>
            <button
                type="button"
                class="notif-row__action"
                ng-show="notification.sticky == 1 && notification.showUN == 0"
                ng-click="$event.stopPropagation(); toggleStickyValue();"
                data-toggle="tooltip"
                data-placement="top"
                title="Unpin"
                aria-label="Unpin"
            >
                <svg aria-hidden="true"><use href="/cachedStatic/iconUrl1?file=%2Fthemes%2Fmpa%2Fassets%2Fsvg%2Fcommon-svg%2Ficons-sprite.svg&hash=qhdR2R0QVhhpU_2uFWEE#pin-off"></use></svg>            </button>
            <button
                type="button"
                class="notif-row__action"
                ng-show="notification.sticky == 0"
                ng-click="$event.stopPropagation(); toggleStickyValue();"
                data-toggle="tooltip"
                data-placement="top"
                title="Pin"
                aria-label="Pin"
            >
                <svg aria-hidden="true"><use href="/cachedStatic/iconUrl1?file=%2Fthemes%2Fmpa%2Fassets%2Fsvg%2Fcommon-svg%2Ficons-sprite.svg&hash=qhdR2R0QVhhpU_2uFWEE#pin"></use></svg>            </button>
        </div>

        <div class="notif-row__timestamp">{{notification.date | timeAgo}}</div>
    </div>
</div>
</script>

          </div>

          </timer-input>

               >
    </div>

    <!-- Category Tabs -->
    <div class="crm-actions-panel__tabs">
        <button class="crm-actions-panel__tab"
                ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__tab--active': activeTab === 'all'}"
                ng-click="setActiveTab('all')"
                type="button">
            All <span class="crm-actions-panel__tab-count">{{totalVisibleCount}}</span>
        </button>
        <button ng-repeat="cat in orderedCategories"
                class="crm-actions-panel__tab"
                ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__tab--active': activeTab === cat.key}"
                ng-click="setActiveTab(cat.key)"
                ng-if="cat.totalCount > 0"
                type="button">
            <i class="crm-actions-panel__tab-icon" ng-class="cat.tabIconClass"></i>
            {{cat.label}} <span class="crm-actions-panel__tab-count">{{cat.visibleCount}}</span>
        </button>
    </div>

    <!-- Scrollable Content Area -->
    <div class="crm-actions-panel__content">

        <!-- "All" view: grouped by category with section headers -->
        <div ng-if="activeTab === 'all'">
            <div ng-repeat="cat in orderedCategories"
                 ng-if="cat.visibleCount > 0"
                 class="crm-actions-panel__section">

                <!-- Section header: colored dot + label -->
                <div class="crm-actions-panel__section-header">
                    <span class="crm-actions-panel__section-dot"></span>
                    {{cat.label}}
                </div>

                <!-- Card grid for this section -->
                <div class="crm-actions-panel__grid">
                    <ng-container ng-repeat="item in cat.visibleItems track by item.key">
                        <!-- Action Card: renders a single action item in the card grid -->
<!-- Expects `item` from ng-repeat scope with: type, visible, url, iconClass, label, modalOptions, buttonOptions, key -->

<!-- Link type -->
<a ng-if="item.type == 'link' && item.visible !== false"
   href="{{item.url}}"
   class="crm-actions-panel__card"
   ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
   ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
   ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
   ng-click="closePanel()">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</a>

<!-- Modal type -->
<a ng-if="item.type == 'modal' && item.visible !== false"
   href="#"
   class="crm-actions-panel__card"
   ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
   ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
   ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
   ng-click="openModal(item)">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</a>

<!-- Confirm button type -->
<button ng-if="item.type == 'confirmButton' && item.visible !== false"
        class="crm-actions-panel__card"
        ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
        ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
        ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
        sd-modal-confirm
        ng-attr-action-url="{{item.url}}"
        config="{title: '{{item.buttonOptions.confirmText}}'}"
        type="button"
        aria-label="{{item.label}}">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</button>

<!-- Copy text type -->
<button ng-if="item.type == 'copyTextButton' && item.visible !== false"
        class="crm-actions-panel__card"
        ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
        ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
        ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
        auto-select="{copy:true,copySuccess:'{{item.buttonOptions.copySuccess}}',copyFailure:'{{item.buttonOptions.copyFailure}}'}"
        copy-text="{{item.buttonOptions.copyText}}"
        type="button"
        aria-label="{{item.label}}">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</button>
                    </ng-container>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Single category view: flat grid, no headers -->
        <div ng-if="activeTab !== 'all'" class="crm-actions-panel__grid">
            <ng-container ng-repeat="cat in orderedCategories">
                <ng-container ng-if="activeTab === cat.key">
                    <ng-container ng-repeat="item in cat.visibleItems track by item.key">
                        <!-- Action Card: renders a single action item in the card grid -->
<!-- Expects `item` from ng-repeat scope with: type, visible, url, iconClass, label, modalOptions, buttonOptions, key -->

<!-- Link type -->
<a ng-if="item.type == 'link' && item.visible !== false"
   href="{{item.url}}"
   class="crm-actions-panel__card"
   ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
   ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
   ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
   ng-click="closePanel()">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</a>

<!-- Modal type -->
<a ng-if="item.type == 'modal' && item.visible !== false"
   href="#"
   class="crm-actions-panel__card"
   ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
   ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
   ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
   ng-click="openModal(item)">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</a>

<!-- Confirm button type -->
<button ng-if="item.type == 'confirmButton' && item.visible !== false"
        class="crm-actions-panel__card"
        ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
        ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
        ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
        sd-modal-confirm
        ng-attr-action-url="{{item.url}}"
        config="{title: '{{item.buttonOptions.confirmText}}'}"
        type="button"
        aria-label="{{item.label}}">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</button>

<!-- Copy text type -->
<button ng-if="item.type == 'copyTextButton' && item.visible !== false"
        class="crm-actions-panel__card"
        ng-class="{'crm-actions-panel__card--focused': focusedItemKey === item.key}"
        ng-mouseenter="setFocusedItem(item.key)"
        ng-mouseleave="clearFocusedItem()"
        auto-select="{copy:true,copySuccess:'{{item.buttonOptions.copySuccess}}',copyFailure:'{{item.buttonOptions.copyFailure}}'}"
        copy-text="{{item.buttonOptions.copyText}}"
        type="button"
        aria-label="{{item.label}}">
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-icon"><i ng-class="item.iconClass"></i></span>
    <span class="crm-actions-panel__card-label">{{item.label}}</span>
</button>
                    </ng-container>
                </ng-container>
            </ng-container>
        </div>

        <!-- Empty state -->
        <div ng-if="totalVisibleCount === 0" class="crm-actions-panel__empty">
            No actions found        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Footer -->
    <div class="crm-actions-panel__footer">
        <span class="crm-actions-panel__footer-count">
            <span class="crm-actions-panel__footer-badge">{{totalVisibleCount}}</span> actions available        </span>
        <div class="crm-actions-panel__footer-shortcuts">
            <span><kbd>esc</kbd> close</span>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
</script>
